<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in; background-color: white">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">Management&#8217;s
unaudited estimate of the range of the net asset value per share of our common stock as of December&#160;31, 2024 was between $8.33 and $8.43.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">In addition, for
the quarter ended December&#160;31, 2024, management's unaudited estimate of the range of our net investment income was between $0.23 and $0.27 per share of our common stock and management's unaudited estimate of the range of our realized losses was between $0.14 and $0.10 per
share of our common stock.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>
